2021-02-02 16:46:26.796 +03:00 [Information] [Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command] [{ Id: 20101, Name: "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command.CommandExecuted" }] Executed DbCommand ("455"ms) [Parameters=["@__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)"], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']"
""SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CategoryType], [t].[CreaDate], [t].[CreaUser], [t].[Definition], [t].[IsActive], [t].[IsDeleted], [t].[IsState], [t].[IsStatus], [t].[ModDate], [t].[ModUser], [t].[Name], [t].[OrderNo], [t].[PublishDate], [t].[PublishDuration], [t0].[Id], [t0].[CreaDate], [t0].[CreaUser], [t0].[Definition], [t0].[IsActive], [t0].[IsDeleted], [t0].[IsState], [t0].[IsStatus], [t0].[ModDate], [t0].[ModUser], [t0].[Name], [t0].[OrderNo], [t0].[WorkshopId]
FROM (
    SELECT [w].[Id], [w].[CategoryType], [w].[CreaDate], [w].[CreaUser], [w].[Definition], [w].[IsActive], [w].[IsDeleted], [w].[IsState], [w].[IsStatus], [w].[ModDate], [w].[ModUser], [w].[Name], [w].[OrderNo], [w].[PublishDate], [w].[PublishDuration]
    FROM [Workshop] AS [w]
    WHERE [w].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreaDate], [s].[CreaUser], [s].[Definition], [s].[IsActive], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[IsState], [s].[IsStatus], [s].[ModDate], [s].[ModUser], [s].[Name], [s].[OrderNo], [s].[WorkshopId]
    FROM [Section] AS [s]

""SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CreaDate], [t].[CreaUser], [t].[Definition], [t].[IsActive], [t].[IsDeleted], [t].[IsState], [t].[IsStatus], [t].[ModDate], [t].[ModUser], [t].[Name], [t].[OrderNo], [t].[WorkshopId], [t0].[Id], [t0].[CategoryType], [t0].[CreaDate], [t0].[CreaUser], [t0].[Definition], [t0].[IsActive], [t0].[IsDeleted], [t0].[IsState], [t0].[IsStatus], [t0].[ModDate], [t0].[ModUser], [t0].[Name], [t0].[OrderNo], [t0].[PublishDate], [t0].[PublishDuration]

    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CreaDate], [s].[CreaUser], [s].[Definition], [s].[IsActive], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[IsState], [s].[IsStatus], [s].[ModDate], [s].[ModUser], [s].[Name], [s].[OrderNo], [s].[WorkshopId]

    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [w].[Id], [w].[CategoryType], [w].[CreaDate], [w].[CreaUser], [w].[Definition], [w].[IsActive], [w].[IsDeleted], [w].[IsState], [w].[IsStatus], [w].[ModDate], [w].[ModUser], [w].[Name], [w].[OrderNo], [w].[PublishDate], [w].[PublishDuration]
